NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING 
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES 
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER 
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By  Order)
Director  of  Stationery  and  Printing.

Public Notice
M.S. Suresh a Male Child, born to Thiru Sankaran M.K. on 29th January 1964, residing at 20/6, Rajnaicker 
Thottam, Kuniamuthur, Coimbatore-641 008, has been living as a Female after an elaborate sexual reassignment surgery 
by Dr. S. Natarajan MS, Reg. No.39523, Coimbatore Medical College Hospital, Coimbatore-641 018. By this I, may be 
treated as a Female and shall henceforth be known as Shivani.
Coimbatore,	
	
M.S. SURESH
24th May 2019.
